Remove <script>...</script> tags and their content\n    #    Loop to handle nested/malformed script tags\n    prev = None\n    while prev != content:\n        prev = content\n        content = re.sub(r'<script\\b[^>]*>[\\s\\S]*?</script\\s*>', '', content, flags=re.IGNORECASE)\n    # Remove any remaining orphan script tags\n    content = re.sub(r'</?script\\b[^>]*/?>', '', content, flags=re.IGNORECASE)\n\n    # 2. Remove <script>...</script> tags and their content\n    prev = None\n    while prev != content:\n        prev = content\n        content = re.sub(r'<script\\b[^>]*>[\\s\\S]*?</script\\s*>', '', content, flags=re.IGNORECASE)\n    # Remove any remaining orphan script tags\n    content = re.sub(r'</?script\\b[^>]*/?>', '', content, flags=re.IGNORECASE)\n\n    # 2. Remove dangerous container tags and their content\n    for tag in ['iframe', 'object', 'embed', 'applet', 'math', 'base',\n                'svg', 'meta', 'xss', 'isindex']:\n        prev = None\n        while prev != content:\n            prev = content\n            content = re.sub(\n                rf'<{tag}\\b[^>]*>[\\s\\S]*?</{tag}\\s*>',\n                '', content, flags=re.IGNORECASE\n            )\n        content = re.sub(rf'</?{tag}\\b[^>]*/?>', '', content, flags=re.IGNORECASE)\n\n    # 3. Neutralize javascript:/vbscript:/data: in URL attributes\n    def _clean_url_attr(match):\n        attr_name = match.group(1)\n        quote = match.group(2) or ''\n        value = match.group(3)\n        end_quote = match.group(4) or ''\n\n        if value is not None:\n            decoded = _decode_and_strip(value)\n            if re.match(r'(?:javascript|vbscript|livescript)\\s*:', decoded):\n                return attr_name + quote + end_quote\n            if re.match(r'data\\s*:', decoded) and 'text/html' in decoded:\n                return attr_name + quote + end_quote\n\n        return match.group(0)\n\n    url_attrs = r'(?:href|src|action|formaction|poster|background|dynsrc|lowsrc|xlink:href)'\n    content = re.sub(\n        rf'({url_attrs}\\s*=\\s*)([\\\"\\']?)((?:(?!\\2).)*?)(\\2)',\n        _clean_url_attr,\n        content,\n        flags=re.IGNORECASE\n    )\n\n    # Also handle unquoted URL attributes\n    content = re.sub(\n        rf'({url_attrs}\\s*=\\s*)([^\\s\"\\'>]+)',\n        lambda m: _clean_url_attr(\n            type('M', (), {\n                'group': lambda self, n: {\n                    0: m.group(0), 1: m.group(1),\n                    2: '', 3: m.group(2), 4: ''\n                }[n]\n            })()\n        ),\n        content,\n        flags=re.IGNORECASE\n    )\n\n    # 5. Remove <script>...</script> tags and their content\n    prev = None\n    while prev != content:\n        prev = content\n        content = re.sub(r'<script\\b[^>]*>[\\s\\S]*?</script\\s*>', '', content, flags=re.IGNORECASE)\n    # Remove any remaining orphan script tags\n    content = re.sub(r'</?script\\b[^>]*/?>', '', content, flags=re.IGNORECASE)\n\n    # 2. Remove dangerous container tags and their content\n    for tag in ['iframe', 'object', 'embed', 'applet', 'math', 'base',\n                'svg', 'meta', 'xss', 'isindex']:\n        prev = None\n        while prev != content:\n            prev = content\n            content = re.sub(\n                rf'<{tag}\\b[^>]*>[\\s\\S]*?</{tag}\\s*>',\n                '', content, flags=re.IGNORECASE\n            )\n        content = re.sub(rf'</?{tag}\\b[^>]*/?>', '', content, flags=re.IGNORECASE)\n\n    # 3. Remove ALL event handler attributes (on*)\n    content = re.sub(\n        r'[\\s/]+on\\w+\\s*=\\s*(?:\"[^\"]*\"|\\'[^\\']*\\'|`[^`]*`|[^\\s;>]*;?)',\n        '', content, flags=re.IGNORECASE\n    )\n    # Handle event handlers immediately after a quote (no whitespace separator)\n    content = re.sub(\n        r'(?<=[\"\\'])on\\w+\\s*=\\s*(?:\"[^\"]*\"|\\'[^\\']*\\'|[^\\s>]*)',\n        '', content, flags=re.IGNORECASE\n    )\n\n    # 4. Neutralize javascript:/vbscript:/data: URLs in attributes\n    #    Handle double-quoted attribute values\n    def _clean_quoted_url(match):\n        prefix = match.group(1)  # e.g. href=\n        quote = match.group(2)   # \" or '\n        value = match.group(3)   # the URL value\n        if _is_dangerous_url(value):\n            return prefix + quote + quote  # empty the value\n        return match.group(0)\n\n    url_attr_names = r'(?:href|src|action|formaction|poster|background|dynsrc|lowsrc|xlink:href)'\n\n    # Quoted values (double or single quotes)\n    content = re.sub(\n        rf'({url_attr_names}\\s*=\\s*)([\"\\'])([\\s\\S]*?)\\2',\n        _clean_quoted_url,\n        content,\n        flags=re.IGNORECASE\n    )\n\n    # Unquoted values\n    def _clean_unquoted_url(match):\n        prefix = match.group(1)\n        value = match.group(2)\n        if _is_dangerous_url(value):\n            return prefix + '\"\"'\n        return match.group(0)\n\n    content = re.sub(\n        rf'({url_attr_names}\\s*=\\s*)([^\\s\"\\'>]+)',\n        _clean_unquoted_url,\n        content,\n        flags=re.IGNORECASE\n    )\n\n    # 5. Remove style attributes containing javascript/expression/entity-encoded content\n    def _clean_style_attr(match):\n        quote = match.group(2)\n        value = match.group(3)\n        if value:\n            decoded = html.unescape(value).lower()\n            if re.search(r'(?:javascript|expression|vbscript|behavior)', decoded):\n                return ''\n            if re.search(r'url\\s*\\(', decoded):\n                inner = re.search(r'url\\s*\\(\\s*[\"\\']?\\s*(.*?)\\s*[\"\\']?\\s*\\)', decoded)\n                if inner and re.match(r'(?:javascript|vbscript|data)\\s*:', inner.group(1).strip()):\n                    return ''\n            if '&#' in value:\n                return ''\n        return match.group(0)\n\n    content = re.sub(\n        r'(style\\s*=\\s*)([\"\\'])([\\s\\S]*?)\\2',\n        _clean_style_attr,\n        content,\n        flags=re.IGNORECASE\n    )\n\n    # 6. Remove ALL event handler attributes (on*)\n    content = re.sub(\n        r'[\\s/]+on\\w+\\s*=\\s*(?:\"[^\"]*\"|\\'[^\\']*\\'|`[^`]*`|[^\\s;>]*;?)',\n        '', content, flags=re.IGNORECASE\n    )\n    # Handle event handlers immediately after a quote (no whitespace separator)\n    content = re.sub(\n        r'(?<=[\"\\'])on\\w+\\s*=\\s*(?:\"[^\"]*\"|\\'[^\\']*\\'|[^\\s>]*)',\n        '', content, flags=re.IGNORECASE\n    )\n\n    # 4. Neutralize javascript:/vbscript:/data: URLs in attributes\n    #    Handle double-quoted attribute values\n    def _clean_quoted_url(match):\n        prefix = match.group(1)  # e.g. href=\n        quote = match.group(2)   # \" or '\n        value = match.group(3)   # the URL value\n        if _is_dangerous_url(value):\n            return prefix + quote + quote  # empty the value\n        return match.group(0)\n\n    url_attr_names = r'(?:href|src|action|formaction|poster|background|dynsrc|lowsrc|xlink:href)'\n\n    # Quoted values (double or single quotes)\n    content = re.sub(\n        rf'({url_attr_names}\\s*=\\s*)([\"\\'])([\\s\\S]*?)\\2',\n        _clean_quoted_url,\n        content,\n        flags=re.IGNORECASE\n    )\n\n    # Unquoted values\n    def _clean_unquoted_url(match):\n        prefix = match.group(1)\n        value = match.group(2)\n        if _is_dangerous_url(value):\n            return prefix + '\"\"'\n        return match.group(0)\n\n    content = re.sub(\n        rf'({url_attr_names}\\s*=\\s*)([^\\s\"\\'>]+)',\n        _clean_unquoted_url,\n        content,\n        flags=re.IGNORECASE\n    )\n\n    # 5. Remove style attributes containing javascript/expression/entity-encoded content\n    def _clean_style_attr(match):\n        quote = match.group(2)\n        value = match.group(3)\n        if value:\n            decoded = html.unescape(value).lower()\n            if re.search(r'(?:javascript|expression|vbscript|behavior)', decoded):\n                return ''\n            if re.search(r'url\\s*\\(', decoded):\n                inner = re.search(r'url\\s*\\(\\s*[\"\\']?\\s*(.*?)\\s*[\"\\']?\\s*\\)', decoded)\n                if inner and re.match(r'(?:javascript|vbscript|data)\\s*:', inner.group(1).strip()):\n                    return ''\n            if '&#' in value:\n                return ''\n        return match.group(0)\n\n    content = re.sub(\n        r'(style\\s*=\\s*)([\"\\'])([\\s\\S]*?)\\2',\n        _clean_style_attr,\n        content,\n        flags=re.IGNORECASE\n    )\n\n    # 6. Remove <style> blocks containing dangerous content\n    def _clean_style_block(match):\n        style_content = match.group(1)\n        decoded = html.unescape(style_content).lower()\n        if re.search(r'(?:javascript|expression|vbscript|behavior)', decoded):\n            return ''\n        return match.group(0)\n\n    content = re.sub(\n        r'<style\\b[^>]*>([\\s\\S]*?)</style\\s*>',\n        _clean_style_block,\n        content,\n        flags=re.IGNORECASE\n    )\n\n    # 7. Remove <link> tags with dangerous URLs\n    content = re.sub(\n        r'<link\\b[^>]*(?:javascript|vbscript)[^>]*/?>',\n        '', content, flags=re.IGNORECASE\n    )\n\n    return content\n\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    if len(sys.argv) < 2:\n        print(\"Usage: python filter.py <html_file>\", file=sys.stderr)\n        sys.exit(1)\n\n    filepath = sys.argv[1]\n    with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8', errors='replace') as f:\n        content = f.read()\n\n    filtered = filter_xss(content)\n\n    with open(filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n        f.write(filtered)\n"}}
